# Concept-usage audit — mod localization

One-shot semantic audit of every game-concept reference in `localization/english/*.yml`. Generated by `scripts/analysis/concept_usage_inventory.py` + `render_concept_usage_audit.py`.

**Purpose.** Victoria 3 links concepts only via the explicit forms `[concept_X]` and `[Concept('concept_X','display')]` (no plain-text auto-linking — vanilla concepts define no aliases). This audit checks whether each reference's *meaning* fits its surrounding text. It complements `concept_reference_audit.py`, which only checks that a referenced concept *exists* (unregistered refs spam the engine log); the references here all exist but some link the wrong meaning — e.g. "genetic `[concept_screening]`" links the **naval ship-screening** concept.

**Method.** Judgment is concentrated on the *ambiguity watchlist* — concepts whose display name is a common English word (listed below). Every instance of a watchlist concept was read. Concepts with a Vic3-specific name (`concept_gdp`, `concept_bureaucracy`, …) cannot be confused with another meaning and are marked **valid (unambiguous)**.

## Summary

- **2840** reference instances audited (**24** misuses fixed this pass → plain text; **2816** remain in the live inventory below).
- Live: `[concept_X]` 2378, `[Concept(...)]` 438, across **252** distinct concepts.
- **24 misuses** (fixed) + **29 borderline** instances (kept), the latter including all 23 `concept_obligation` uses.
- `$concept_X$` free-standing substitutions (188) are loc variables, not links — excluded.

## Ambiguity watchlist

Concepts whose display name is a common English word; every instance of each was read. Count is the **pre-fix** total (live + fixed).

| Concept | Display name | Vic3 meaning | Confusable with |
|---|---|---|---|
| `concept_institution` (84) | Institution | A government Institution | educational/financial institution |
| `concept_heir` (51) | Heir | The dynastic Heir | metaphorical heir/legacy |
| `concept_homeland` (32) | Homeland | A culture's Homeland state | homeland generally |
| `concept_amendment` (29) | Amendment | An Amendment to a law | constitutional amendment |
| `concept_radical` (25) | Radical | A Radical (a dissatisfied/radicalized pop) | the adjective 'radical' (extreme/revolutionary) |
| `concept_obligation` (23) | Obligation | A diplomatic favor owed (from diplo plays/buyouts) | treaty/legal/debt 'obligations' generally |
| `concept_authority` (18) | Authority | The Authority resource | governmental authority / an expert |
| `concept_pop` (17) | Pop | A population group (Pop) | pop culture / pop-up |
| `concept_turmoil` (17) | Turmoil | State Turmoil | emotional turmoil |
| `concept_country` (16) | Country | A Country | countryside |
| `concept_state` (10) | State | An administrative State region | nation/condition/government |
| `concept_detection` (7) | Detection | Covert-op/naval Detection | general detection |
| `concept_screening` (6) | Screening | Naval ship-screening (counters ship vulnerability) | medical/genetic/psychological/personnel screening |
| `concept_fervor` (6) | Fervor | Cultural national-spirit stat (drives assimilation) | emotional intensity: religious/patriotic/speculative fervor |
| `concept_escalation` (6) | Escalation | Diplomatic-play Escalation | general escalation |
| `concept_bolster` (4) | Bolster | The Bolster action on a political movement | the plain verb 'to bolster' (strengthen) |
| `concept_law` (4) | Law | An enacted government Law | law of nature / rule of law |
| `concept_defense` (4) | Defense | Unit combat Defense stat | legal/self/civil defense |
| `concept_offense` (4) | Offense | Unit combat Offense stat | taking offense / criminal offense |
| `concept_loyalist` (4) | Loyalist | A Loyalist pop | political loyalist generally |
| `concept_innovation` (3) | Innovation | The Innovation (research) resource | general innovation |
| `concept_construction` (3) | Construction | The Construction system | general construction |
| `concept_profession` (3) | Profession | A pop Profession | general profession |
| `concept_prominence` (2) | Prominence | A character's political prominence stat | 'rise to prominence' (general fame) |
| `concept_influence` (2) | Influence | The diplomatic Influence resource | general influence |
| `concept_culture` (2) | Culture | A Culture group | the arts / corporate culture |
| `concept_acceptance` (2) | Acceptance | Cultural Acceptance | general acceptance |
| `concept_dominion` (1) | Dominion | Subject type (autonomous vassal) | 'dominion' as realm/domain |
| `concept_market` (1) | Market | The economic Market | labour/stock/flea market |
| `concept_subject` (1) | Subject | A diplomatic Subject (vassal) | topic / person / 'subject to' |
| `concept_unit` (1) | Military Unit | A military Unit | unit of measure/account |
| `concept_company` (1) | Company | A chartered Company | military company / companionship |
| `concept_building` (1) | Building | An economic Building | the gerund 'building' |
| `concept_conversion` (1) | Conversion | Religious Conversion of pops | unit/building conversion |
| `concept_clout` (1) | Clout | An interest group's Clout | general clout |
| `concept_occupancy` (1) | Occupancy | How fully a building is staffed | military occupation / tenancy |

All `concept_obligation` instances are flagged borderline: the concept is specifically a diplomatic favor owed (from diplo plays / buyouts), but every mod use means a treaty / debt / legal "obligation" in the generic sense. Low-stakes (the word is generic) — reported, not fixed.

## Full inventory

Every reference, grouped by concept (descending frequency). Verdict column: `valid (unambiguous)` = Vic3-specific name; `valid` = watchlist concept, read and confirmed correct; `misuse`/`borderline` as above.
